        <script>
         try{
						var marqueesHeight1 = 30;
						var stopscroll1= false;

						var scrollElem1 = document.getElementById("icefable1");
						with(scrollElem1){
							style.height = marqueesHeight1;
							style.overflow = 'hidden';
							noWrap = true;
						}
						scrollElem1.onmouseover = new Function('stopscroll1 = true');
						scrollElem1.onmouseout  = new Function('stopscroll1 = false');
						var preTop1 = 0;
						var currentTop1 = 0;
						var stoptime1 = 0;
						var leftElem1 = document.getElementById("indexchannel1");
						scrollElem1.appendChild(leftElem1.cloneNode(true));
						init_srolltext1();
					}catch(e){}
					function init_srolltext1(){
						scrollElem1.scrollTop = 0;
						setInterval('scrollUp1()', 20);
					}
					function scrollUp1(){
						if(stopscroll1) return;
						currentTop1 += 1;
						if(currentTop1 == 31) {
							stoptime1 += 1;
							currentTop1 -= 1;
							if(stoptime1 == 180) {	//此处数字越小越快
								currentTop1 = 0;
								stoptime1 = 0;
							}
						}else{
							preTop1 = scrollElem1.scrollTop;
							scrollElem1.scrollTop += 1;
							if(preTop1 == scrollElem1.scrollTop){
								scrollElem1.scrollTop = 0;
								scrollElem1.scrollTop += 1;
							}
						}
					}
					function timestampToTime(timestamp) {
						var date = new Date(timestamp * 1000);
						D = date.getDate();
						if(D<10) D='0'+D;
						h = date.getHours();
						if(h<10) h='0'+h;
						m = date.getMinutes();
						if(m<10) m='0'+m;
						return D+'日 '+h+':'+m;
					}
					function getCookie(name){ 
						var strCookie=document.cookie; 
						var arrCookie=strCookie.split("; "); 
						for(var i=0;i<arrCookie.length;i++){ 
						var arr=arrCookie[i].split("="); 
						if(arr[0]==name)return arr[1]; 
						} 
						return ""; 
					} 
					function setCookie(name,value){ 
						var Days = 30; 
						var exp = new Date(); 
						exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + Days*24*60*60*1000); 
						document.cookie = name + "="+ escape (value) + ";path=/;expires=" + exp.toGMTString(); 
					}
					var currTime = new Date();
					var nextTime=0;
					$.ajax({
						type:"GET",
						url:"http://3g.ali213.net/zhuanti/sports/ajaxmatchesbyrange",
						data:{
							activityid:1
						},
						async:false,
						dataType:"jsonp",
						jsonp : 'callback',
						success:function(json){
							for(var i in json.data){
								if(currTime.getTime()/1000<json.data[i]['playtime'] && nextTime<json.data[i]['playtime']){
									$('.wc-c').attr('id',json.data[i]['id']);
									if(getCookie('matchid')==$('.wc-c').attr('id')){
										$('.wc-c-l-f').removeClass('wc-c-click');
										$('.wc-c-r-f').removeClass('wc-c-click');
									}else{
										$('.wc-c-l-f').addClass('wc-c-click');
										$('.wc-c-r-f').addClass('wc-c-click');
									}
									nextTime=json.data[i]['playtime'];
									$('.wc-c-c-f').html(json.data[i]['amounts']/100+'RMB');
									$('.wc-c-c-t').html(timestampToTime(nextTime));
									var gnarr=json.data[i]['candidateids'].split(',');
									$('.wc-c-l-f').attr('id',gnarr[0]);
									$('.wc-c-r-f').attr('id',gnarr[1]);
									$.ajax({
										type:"GET",
										url:"http://3g.ali213.net/zhuanti/sports/ajaxcandidatebyrange",
										data:{
											activityid:1,
											status:1
										},
										async:false,
										dataType:"jsonp",
										jsonp : 'callback',
										success:function(json1){
											for(var j in json1.data){
												if(gnarr[0]==json1.data[j]['id']){
													$('.wc-c-l-c').html(json1.data[j]['name']);
													$('.wc-c-l-t img').attr('src',json1.data[j]['cover']);
												}
												if(gnarr[1]==json1.data[j]['id']){
													$('.wc-c-r-c').html(json1.data[j]['name']);
													$('.wc-c-r-t img').attr('src',json1.data[j]['cover']);
												}
											}
										}
									});
									$.ajax({
										type:"GET",
										url:"http://3g.ali213.net/zhuanti/sports/ajaxsupportrate",
										data:{
											matchid:json.data[i]['id']
										},
										async:false,
										dataType:"jsonp",
										jsonp : 'callback',
										success:function(json2){
											if(json2.data.length>0){
												if(json2.data[0]['optionid']==$('.wc-c-l-f').attr('id')){
													var wr=json2.data[0]['rate'].toFixed(2);

													var wc_k=Math.floor(wr*260);
													var wc_z=Math.floor(wr*100);
													$('.wc-b-k').css('width',wc_k+'px');
													$('.wc-b-k').html(wc_z+'%');
													$('.wc-b-z').css('width',(260-wc_k)+'px');
													$('.wc-b-z').html((100-wc_z)+'%');

													//$('.wc-b-k').css('width',wr*260+'px');
													//$('.wc-b-k').html(wr*100+'%');
													//$('.wc-b-z').css('width',(260-wr*260)+'px');
													//$('.wc-b-z').html((100-wr*100)+'%');
												}else if(json2.data[0]['optionid']==$('.wc-c-r-f').attr('id')){
													var wr=json2.data[0]['rate'].toFixed(2);

													var wc_k=Math.floor(wr*260);
													var wc_z=Math.floor(wr*100);
													$('.wc-b-z').css('width',wc_k+'px');
													$('.wc-b-z').html(wc_z+'%');
													$('.wc-b-k').css('width',(260-wc_k)+'px');
													$('.wc-b-k').html((100-wc_z)+'%');

													//$('.wc-b-z').css('width',wr*260+'px');
													//$('.wc-b-z').html(wr*100+'%');
													//$('.wc-b-k').css('width',(260-wr*260)+'px');
													//$('.wc-b-k').html((100-wr*100)+'%');
												}
											}
										}
									});
									return false;
								}
							}
						}
					});
					$('.wc-c-l,.wc-c-r').on('click','.wc-c-click',function(){
						$.ajax({
							type:"GET",
							url:"http://3g.ali213.net/zhuanti/sports/ajaxsupportting",
							data:{
								matchid:$('.wc-c').attr('id'),
								optionid:$(this).attr('id')
							},
							async:false,
							dataType:"jsonp",
							jsonp : 'callback',
							success:function(json3){
								$('.wc-c-l-f').removeClass('wc-c-click');
								$('.wc-c-r-f').removeClass('wc-c-click');
								setCookie('matchid',$('.wc-c').attr('id'));
								$.ajax({
									type:"GET",
									url:"http://3g.ali213.net/zhuanti/sports/ajaxsupportrate",
									data:{
										matchid:$('.wc-c').attr('id')
									},
									async:false,
									dataType:"jsonp",
									jsonp : 'callback',
									success:function(json2){
										if(json2.data.length>0){
											if(json2.data[0]['optionid']==$('.wc-c-l-f').attr('id')){
												var wr=json2.data[0]['rate'].toFixed(2);
												$('.wc-b-k').css('width',wr*260+'px');
												$('.wc-b-k').html(wr*100+'%');
												$('.wc-b-z').css('width',(260-wr*260)+'px');
												$('.wc-b-z').html((100-wr*100)+'%');
											}else if(json2.data[0]['optionid']==$('.wc-c-r-f').attr('id')){
												var wr=json2.data[0]['rate'].toFixed(2);
												$('.wc-b-z').css('width',wr*260+'px');
												$('.wc-b-z').html(wr*100+'%');
												$('.wc-b-k').css('width',(260-wr*260)+'px');
												$('.wc-b-k').html((100-wr*100)+'%');
											}
										}
									}
								});
							}
						});
					});
        </script>

       <script>
        $(function(){
					var tlen=$('.fybph-con_con li').length;
					//上一个
					$('.fybph-con_prev').click(function(){
						var tl=parseInt($('.fybph-con_con ul').css('left'));
						if(tl<0){
							$('.fybph-con_con ul').css('left',tl+90);
						}
					});
					//下一个
					$('.fybph-con_next').click(function(){
						var tl=parseInt($('.fybph-con_con ul').css('left'));
						if(tl>-(tlen-3)*90){
							$('.fybph-con_con ul').css('left',tl-90);
						}
					});
				});
       </script>

      <script>
       (function(){
                     function CurentTime()
                     { 
                                var now = new Date();
                               
                                var year = now.getFullYear();       //年
                                var month = now.getMonth() + 1;     //月
                                var day = now.getDate();            //日
                               
                                var hh = now.getHours();            //时
                                var mm = now.getMinutes();          //分
                               
                                var clock = year + "-";
                               
                                if(month < 10)
                                    clock += "0";
                               
                                clock += month + "-";
                               
                                if(day < 10)
                                    clock += "0";
                                   
                                clock += day + " ";
                                return(clock); 
                     } 
                     $(".live_li").bind("mouseover",function(){
                                 $(this).find(".vd_yugao_right_con").hide();    
                                 $(this).find(".vd_yugao_right_btn").show(); 
                     });
                     $(".live_li").bind("mouseout",function(){
                                 $(this).find(".vd_yugao_right_con").show();    
                                 $(this).find(".vd_yugao_right_btn").hide(); 
                     });
                     $(".yugao_li").bind("mouseover",function(){
                                 $(this).find(".m_yugao").attr("style","display:block"); 
                     });
                     $(".yugao_li").bind("mouseout",function(){
                                 $(this).find(".m_yugao").attr("style","display:none");
                     });
                     $(".m_yugao").bind("click",function(){
                                 window.open("http://qzs.qq.com/snsapp/app/bee/widget/open.htm#content="+ encodeURIComponent($(this).parents(".yugao_li").find(".vd_yugao_title").text())+"&time="+encodeURIComponent(CurentTime()+$(this).prev().html())+"&advance=5&url="+encodeURIComponent($(this).parents(".yugao_li").find(".vd_yugao_title a").attr("href")));
                     });
                })()
      </script>
